\index{jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit\+\_\+write@{jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit\+\_\+write}!A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T Descriptor -\/ Clause 7.\+2.\+3@{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T Descriptor -\/ Clause 7.\+2.\+3}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit\+\_\+write(struct jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit const $\ast$p, void $\ast$base, size\+\_\+t pos, size\+\_\+t len)}{jdksavdecc_descriptor_audio_unit_write(struct jdksavdecc_descriptor_audio_unit const *p, void *base, size_t pos, size_t len)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static ssize\+\_\+t jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit\+\_\+write (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio\+\_\+unit} const $\ast$}]{p, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{base, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{pos, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{group__descriptor__audio_ga378aaf48d5f066011436e23c2bf4d455}{}\label{group__descriptor__audio_ga378aaf48d5f066011436e23c2bf4d455}
Store the jdksavdecc\+\_\+descriptor\+\_\+audio structure to a network buffer.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Clause 7.\+2.\+3
\end{DoxyItemize}

Bounds checking of the buffer size is done.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em p} & const pointer to descriptor\+\_\+audio structure to read from. \\
\hline
{\em base} & pointer to raw memory buffer to write to. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & offset from base to write the field to; \\
\hline
{\em len} & length of the raw memory buffer; \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
-\/1 if the buffer length is insufficent, otherwise the offset of the octet following the structure in the buffer. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
